*Q1.* 🕐 Zoya's music lesson starts at 7 o'clock. What time is 1 hour later?
A) 8 o'clock
B) 6 o'clock
C) 7 o'clock
D) 9 o'clock
✅ *Answer:* A) 8 o'clock
💡 One hour after 7 o'clock is 8 o'clock.

*Q1549.* 🕐 Rohan's train leaves at 8 o'clock. What time was it 1 hour earlier?
A) 7 o'clock
B) 6 o'clock
C) 8 o'clock
D) 5 o'clock
✅ *Answer:* A) 7 o'clock
💡 One hour before 8 o'clock is 7 o'clock.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q1550.* 🕐 Kiara's movie starts at 9 o'clock. What time was it 1 hour earlier?
A) 7 o'clock
B) 6 o'clock
C) 8 o'clock
D) 9 o'clock
✅ *Answer:* C) 8 o'clock
💡 One hour before 9 o'clock is 8 o'clock.

*Q1551.* 📈 Arranged smallest → greatest, which comes FIRST? 59, 31, 50
A) 32
B) 59
C) 31
D) 50
✅ *Answer:* C) 31
💡 Ascending order starts with 31.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q1552.* 📅 Aman's match is on Wednesday. Which day comes just before?
A) Thursday
B) Monday
C) Sunday
D) Tuesday
✅ *Answer:* D) Tuesday
💡 Before Wednesday comes Tuesday.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q1553.* 🕐 What time is 2 hours BEFORE 3 o'clock?
A) 4 o'clock
B) 2 o'clock
C) 1 o'clock
D) 3 o'clock
✅ *Answer:* C) 1 o'clock
💡 2 hour(s) before 3 o'clock is 1 o'clock.
